### src\pages\Login\components\EnterOTPCode.tsx
```tsx
import React, { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";

interface EnterOTPCodeProps {
  onClose: () => void;
}

const EnterOTPCode: React.FC<EnterOTPCodeProps> = ({ onClose }) => {
  const [otp, setOtp] = useState<string[]>(["", "", "", "", ""]);
  const [countdown, setCountdown] = useState(56);
  const inputRefs = useRef<(HTMLInputElement | null)[]>([]);

  // Countdown timer
  useEffect(() => {
    if (countdown > 0) {
      const timer = setTimeout(() => setCountdown(countdown - 1), 1000);
      return () => clearTimeout(timer);
    }
  }, [countdown]);

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω thay ƒë·ªïi input OTP
  const handleOtpChange = (index: number, value: string) => {
    // Ch·ªâ cho ph√©p nh·∫≠p s·ªë
    if (!/^\d*$/.test(value)) return;

    const newOtp = [...otp];
    newOtp[index] = value;
    setOtp(newOtp);

    // T·ª± ƒë·ªông chuy·ªÉn sang √¥ ti·∫øp theo
    if (value && index < 4) {
      inputRefs.current[index + 1]?.focus();
    }
  };

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω ph√≠m Backspace
  const handleKeyDown = (index: number, e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === "Backspace" && !otp[index] && index > 0) {
      inputRefs.current[index - 1]?.focus();
    }
  };

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω paste
  const handlePaste = (e: React.ClipboardEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const pastedData = e.clipboardData.getData("text").slice(0, 5);
    const newOtp = pastedData.split("").concat(Array(5).fill("")).slice(0, 5);
    setOtp(newOtp);

    // Focus v√†o √¥ cu·ªëi c√πng c√≥ d·ªØ li·ªáu
    const lastFilledIndex = Math.min(pastedData.length - 1, 4);
    inputRefs.current[lastFilledIndex]?.focus();
  };

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω submit
  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const otpCode = otp.join("");

    if (otpCode.length !== 5) {
      alert("Vui l√≤ng nh·∫≠p ƒë·∫ßy ƒë·ªß m√£ OTP!");
      return;
    }

    // TODO: X·ª≠ l√Ω x√°c th·ª±c OTP
    alert(`M√£ OTP ƒë√£ nh·∫≠p: ${otpCode}`);
    onClose();
  };

  // G·ª≠i l·∫°i m√£ OTP
  const handleResendOTP = () => {
    setCountdown(56);
    setOtp(["", "", "", "", ""]);
    inputRefs.current[0]?.focus();
    // TODO: G·ªçi API g·ª≠i l·∫°i OTP
    alert("ƒê√£ g·ª≠i l·∫°i m√£ OTP!");
  };

  // Format th·ªùi gian countdown
  const formatTime = (seconds: number) => {
    const mins = Math.floor(seconds / 60);
    const secs = seconds % 60;
    return `${mins.toString().padStart(2, "0")}:${secs
      .toString()
      .padStart(2, "0")}`;
  };

  return (
    <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6 w-[400px] relative">
      {/* N√∫t ƒë√≥ng popup */}
      <button
        onClick={onClose}
        className="absolute top-4 right-4 text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-900 font-bold text-xl"
        aria-label="ƒê√≥ng"
      >
        ‚úï
      </button>

      <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-2 text-center">Qu√™n m·∫≠t kh·∫©u</h3>

      <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-6 text-center">Nh·∫≠p m√£ OTP</p>

      <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-6">
        {/* 5 √¥ nh·∫≠p OTP */}
        <div className="flex justify-center space-x-3">
          {otp.map((digit, index) => (
            <input
              key={index}
              ref={(el) => (inputRefs.current[index] = el)}
              type="text"
              maxLength={1}
              value={digit}
              onChange={(e) => handleOtpChange(index, e.target.value)}
              onKeyDown={(e) => handleKeyDown(index, e)}
              onPaste={index === 0 ? handlePaste : undefined}
              className="w-12 h-12 text-center text-lg font-semibold border-2 border-gray-300 rounded-lg focus:border-[#2A9D8F] focus:outline-none transition-colors"
              autoComplete="off"
            />
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* N√∫t x√°c nh·∫≠n */}
        <button
          type="submit"
          className="w-full py-3 bg-[#2A9D8F] text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-[#228B7E] transition-colors font-medium"
        >
          X√°c nh·∫≠n
        </button>

        {/* G·ª≠i l·∫°i m√£ OTP */}
        <div className="text-center">
          {countdown > 0 ? (
            <p className="text-sm text-gray-600">
              G·ª≠i l·∫°i m√£ sau ({formatTime(countdown)})
            </p>
          ) : (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={handleResendOTP}
              className="text-sm text-[#2A9D8F] hover:underline font-medium"
            >
              G·ª≠i l·∫°i m√£ OTP
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
};

export default EnterOTPCode;

```

```tsx
import React, { useState } from "react";
import EnterOTPCode from "./EnterOTPCode";

interface ForgotPasswordProps {

const ForgotPassword: React.FC<ForgotPasswordProps> = ({ onClose }) => {

  const [enterOtpCode, setEnterOtpCode] = useState(false);

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    // Ki·ªÉm tra email c√≥ h·ª£p l·ªá kh√¥ng
    if (!email.trim()) {
      alert("Vui l√≤ng nh·∫≠p email!");
      return;
    }

    // TODO: X·ª≠ l√Ω g·ª≠i email kh√¥i ph·ª•c m·∫≠t kh·∫©u ·ªü ƒë√¢y
    // Gi·∫£ s·ª≠ API call th√†nh c√¥ng

    // Hi·ªÉn th·ªã modal EnterOTPCode thay v√¨ ƒë√≥ng modal hi·ªán t·∫°i
    setEnterOtpCode(true);

    // Kh√¥ng g·ªçi onClose() ·ªü ƒë√¢y n·ªØa
    // onClose(); // ‚Üê X√≥a d√≤ng n√†y
  };

  return (
    <>
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-lg p-6 w-[400px] relative">
        {/* N√∫t ƒë√≥ng popup */}
        <button
          onClick={onClose}
          className="absolute top-4 right-4 text-gray-600 hover:text-gray-900 font-bold"
          aria-label="ƒê√≥ng"
        >
          ‚úï
        </button>

        <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4 text-center">
          Qu√™n m·∫≠t kh·∫©u
        </h3>
        <p className="text-x2 text-[#323333] mb-4 text-center">
          Vui l√≤ng nh·∫≠p email c·ªßa b·∫°n
        </p>

        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
          {/* Tr∆∞·ªùng nh·∫≠p email */}
          <div className="relative">
            <input
              type="email"
              placeholder="Email c·ªßa b·∫°n"
              className="w-full px-4 py-2 border rounded-md"
              value={email}
              onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
              required
            />
          </div>

          {/* N√∫t submit */}
          <button
            type="submit"
            className="w-full py-3 bg-[#2A9D8F] text-white rounded-md hover:bg-[#228B7E] transition"
          >
            G·ª≠i m√£ OTP
          </button>
        </form>
      </div>

      {/* Modal nh·∫≠p m√£ OTP */}
      {enterOtpCode && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/30 backdrop-blur-sm flex justify-center items-center z-50">
          <EnterOTPCode
            onClose={() => {
              setEnterOtpCode(false);
              onClose(); // ƒê√≥ng c·∫£ modal ForgotPassword khi ƒë√≥ng EnterOTPCode
            }}
          />
        </div>
      )}
    </>
  );
};

export default ForgotPassword;
```

### src\pages\Login\hooks\useLoginForm.ts
```ts
// src/pages/Login/hooks/useLoginForm.ts
import { useState } from "react";
import { useDispatch, useSelector } from "react-redux";
import { useNavigate, useLocation } from "react-router-dom";
import { Login, LoginNoRemember } from "../../../store/slices/authSlice";
import type { RootState, AppDispatch } from "../../../store/store";

interface LoginFormData {
  username: string;
  password: string;
  rememberMe: boolean;
}

interface FormErrors {
  username?: string;
  password?: string;
}

export const useLoginForm = () => {
  const dispatch = useDispatch<AppDispatch>();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const location = useLocation();

  const { loading, error, isAuthenticated, user } = useSelector(
    (state: RootState) => state.auth
  );

  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<LoginFormData>({
    username: "",
    password: "",
    rememberMe: false,
  });
  const [formErrors, setFormErrors] = useState<FormErrors>({});
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);

  const handleInputChange = (
    field: keyof LoginFormData,
    value: string | boolean
  ) => {
    setFormData((prev) => ({ ...prev, [field]: value }));

    if (field in formErrors && formErrors[field as keyof FormErrors]) {
      setFormErrors((prev: FormErrors) => ({ ...prev, [field]: undefined }));
    }
  };

  const validateForm = () => {
    const errors: FormErrors = {};

    if (!formData.username) {
      errors.username = "T√™n ƒëƒÉng nh·∫≠p kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ tr·ªëng";
    } else if (formData.username.length < 3) {
      errors.username = "T√™n ƒëƒÉng nh·∫≠p ph·∫£i c√≥ √≠t nh·∫•t 3 k√Ω t·ª±";
    }

    if (!formData.password) {
      errors.password = "M·∫≠t kh·∫©u kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ tr·ªëng";
    } else if (formData.password.length < 6) {
      errors.password = "M·∫≠t kh·∫©u ph·∫£i c√≥ √≠t nh·∫•t 6 k√Ω t·ª±";
    }

    return errors;
  };

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    const errors = validateForm();
    if (Object.keys(errors).length > 0) {
      setFormErrors(errors);
      return;
    }

    try {
      const loginAction = formData.rememberMe ? Login : LoginNoRemember;

      await dispatch(
        loginAction({
          username: formData.username,
          password: formData.password,
        })
      ).unwrap();

      const from = (location.state as any)?.from?.pathname || "/";
      navigate(from, { replace: true });
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error("Login failed:", error);
    }
  };

  return {
    formData,
    formErrors,
    showPassword,
    loading,
    error,
    isAuthenticated,
    user,
    handleInputChange,
    handleSubmit,
    setShowPassword,
  };
};

```

### src\pages\Login\utils\loginValidation.ts
```ts
// utils/loginValidation.ts
interface LoginFormData {
  username: string; // ‚úÖ ƒê·ªïi t·ª´ email sang username
  password: string;
}

interface LoginFormErrors {
  username?: string; // ‚úÖ ƒê·ªïi t·ª´ email sang username
  password?: string;
}

export const validateLogin = (data: LoginFormData): LoginFormErrors => {
  const errors: LoginFormErrors = {};

  // ‚úÖ Validate username thay v√¨ email
  if (!data.username) {
    errors.username = "T√™n ƒëƒÉng nh·∫≠p kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ tr·ªëng";
  } else if (data.username.length < 3) {
    errors.username = "T√™n ƒëƒÉng nh·∫≠p ph·∫£i c√≥ √≠t nh·∫•t 3 k√Ω t·ª±";
  }

  // Validate password
  if (!data.password) {
    errors.password = "M·∫≠t kh·∫©u kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ tr·ªëng";
  } else if (data.password.length < 6) {
    errors.password = "M·∫≠t kh·∫©u ph·∫£i c√≥ √≠t nh·∫•t 6 k√Ω t·ª±";
  }

  return errors;
};
```

### src\pages\Register\index.tsx
```tsx
// pages/Register/index.tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { Eye, EyeOff, User, Mail, Home } from "lucide-react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { useDispatch } from "react-redux";
import type { AppDispatch, RootState } from "@/store/store";
import { register, resetRegisterState } from "@/store/slices/registerSlice";
import { toast } from "react-toastify";
import { useSelector } from "react-redux";

export default function RegisterPage() {
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);
  const [showConfirmPassword, setShowConfirmPassword] = useState(false);

  const [username, setUsername] = useState("");
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
  const [confirmPassword, setConfirmPassword] = useState("");
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState({
    username: "",
    email: "",
    password: "",
    confirmPassword: "",
  });

  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const dispatch = useDispatch<AppDispatch>();

  // L·∫•y state t·ª´ Redux store
  const { loading, success, error, accountData } = useSelector(
    // ‚úÖ Th√™m accountData
    (state: RootState) => state.register
  );

  // Cleanup khi component unmount
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      dispatch(resetRegisterState());
    };
  }, [dispatch]);

  // ‚úÖ C·∫≠p nh·∫≠t x·ª≠ l√Ω khi ƒëƒÉng k√Ω th√†nh c√¥ng
  useEffect(() => {
    if (success && accountData) {
      toast.success(
        "ƒêƒÉng k√Ω t√†i kho·∫£n th√†nh c√¥ng! Ti·∫øp t·ª•c t·∫°o h·ªì s∆° c√° nh√¢n."
      );

      // Truy·ªÅn account data qua state navigation
      setTimeout(() => {
        navigate("/register-customer", {
          state: {
            accountData: accountData,
            fromRegister: true,
          },
        });
      }, 1500);
    }
  }, [success, accountData, navigate]);

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω khi c√≥ l·ªói t·ª´ server
  useEffect(() => {
    if (error) {
      toast.error(error.message);
    }
  }, [error]);

  const validateEmail = (email: string) => {
    return /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email);
  };

  const validatePassword = (password: string) => {
    return /^(?=.*[A-Za-z])(?=.*\d)[A-Za-z\d]{6,}$/.test(password);
  };

  const validateForm = () => {
    const newErrors = {
      username: "",
      email: "",
      password: "",
      confirmPassword: "",
    };
    let isValid = true;

    // Validate username
    if (!username.trim()) {
      newErrors.username = "T√™n ng∆∞·ªùi d√πng kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ tr·ªëng";
      isValid = false;
    } else if (username.trim().length < 3) {
      newErrors.username = "T√™n ng∆∞·ªùi d√πng ph·∫£i c√≥ √≠t nh·∫•t 3 k√Ω t·ª±";
      isValid = false;
    }

    // Validate email
    if (!email.trim()) {
      newErrors.email = "Email kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ tr·ªëng";
      isValid = false;
    } else if (!validateEmail(email)) {
      newErrors.email = "Email kh√¥ng h·ª£p l·ªá";
      isValid = false;
    }

    // Validate password
    if (!password) {
      newErrors.password = "M·∫≠t kh·∫©u kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ tr·ªëng";
      isValid = false;
    } else if (!validatePassword(password)) {
      newErrors.password = "M·∫≠t kh·∫©u ph·∫£i t·ª´ 6 k√Ω t·ª±, g·ªìm ch·ªØ v√† s·ªë";
      isValid = false;
    }

    // Validate confirm password
    if (!confirmPassword) {
      newErrors.confirmPassword = "Vui l√≤ng nh·∫≠p l·∫°i m·∫≠t kh·∫©u";
      isValid = false;
    } else if (password !== confirmPassword) {
      newErrors.confirmPassword = "M·∫≠t kh·∫©u x√°c nh·∫≠n kh√¥ng kh·ªõp";
      isValid = false;
    }

    setErrors(newErrors);
    return isValid;
  };

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    // Validate form tr∆∞·ªõc khi submit
    if (!validateForm()) {
      return;
    }

    // G·ª≠i request ƒëƒÉng k√Ω account
    const registerData = {
      username: username.trim(),
      email: email.trim(),
      password: password,
      confirmPassword: confirmPassword,
      role: "user", // M·∫∑c ƒë·ªãnh l√† user
    };

    try {
      const result = await dispatch(register(registerData));

      if (register.fulfilled.match(result)) {
        // ƒêƒÉng k√Ω th√†nh c√¥ng - useEffect s·∫Ω x·ª≠ l√Ω navigation
        console.log("‚úÖ ƒêƒÉng k√Ω th√†nh c√¥ng:", result.payload);
      } else if (register.rejected.match(result)) {
        // L·ªói t·ª´ server - useEffect s·∫Ω hi·ªÉn th·ªã toast
        console.error("‚ùå ƒêƒÉng k√Ω th·∫•t b·∫°i:", result.payload);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("‚ùå Unexpected error:", error);
      toast.error("C√≥ l·ªói kh√¥ng mong mu·ªën x·∫£y ra");
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex bg-white relative">
      {/* Icon quay v·ªÅ trang homepage */}
      <button
        onClick={() => navigate("/")}
        className="absolute top-4 right-4 text-[#2A9D8F] hover:text-[#228B7E] transition-colors duration-200 z-10"
        title="Quay l·∫°i trang ch√≠nh"
      >
        <Home className="w-6 h-6" />
      </button>

      {/* B√™n ph·∫£i: Form ƒëƒÉng k√Ω */}
      <div className="w-full md:w-1/2 flex items-center justify-center p-8">
        <div className="w-full max-w-sm bg-white p-8 rounded-xl shadow-lg border">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2 text-center">ƒêƒÉng k√Ω</h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-6 text-center">
            T·∫°o t√†i kho·∫£n m·ªõi ƒë·ªÉ b·∫Øt ƒë·∫ßu
          </p>

          <form className="space-y-4" onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
            {/* √î nh·∫≠p username */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                value={username}
                onChange={(e) => setUsername(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="T√™n ng∆∞·ªùi d√πng"
                className={`w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 transition-all duration-200 ${
                  errors.username
                    ? "border-red-500 focus:ring-red-500/20"
                    : "border-gray-300 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]/20 focus:border-[#2A9D8F]"
                }`}
                disabled={loading}
              />
              <User className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
              {errors.username && (
                <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-1">{errors.username}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* √î nh·∫≠p email */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="email"
                value={email}
                onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Email"
                className={`w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 transition-all duration-200 ${
                  errors.email
                    ? "border-red-500 focus:ring-red-500/20"
                    : "border-gray-300 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]/20 focus:border-[#2A9D8F]"
                }`}
                disabled={loading}
              />
              <Mail className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
              {errors.email && (
                <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-1">{errors.email}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* √î nh·∫≠p m·∫≠t kh·∫©u */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type={showPassword ? "text" : "password"}
                value={password}
                onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="M·∫≠t kh·∫©u"
                className={`w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 transition-all duration-200 ${
                  errors.password
                    ? "border-red-500 focus:ring-red-500/20"
                    : "border-gray-300 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]/20 focus:border-[#2A9D8F]"
                }`}
                disabled={loading}
              />
              <div
                onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}
                className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 cursor-pointer text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700 transition-colors"
              >
                {showPassword ? (
                  <EyeOff className="w-5 h-5" />
                ) : (
                  <Eye className="w-5 h-5" />
                )}
              </div>
              {errors.password && (
                <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-1">{errors.password}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* √î nh·∫≠p x√°c nh·∫≠n m·∫≠t kh·∫©u */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type={showConfirmPassword ? "text" : "password"}
                value={confirmPassword}
                onChange={(e) => setConfirmPassword(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Nh·∫≠p l·∫°i m·∫≠t kh·∫©u"
                className={`w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 transition-all duration-200 ${
                  errors.confirmPassword
                    ? "border-red-500 focus:ring-red-500/20"
                    : "border-gray-300 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]/20 focus:border-[#2A9D8F]"
                }`}
                disabled={loading}
              />
              <div
                onClick={() => setShowConfirmPassword(!showConfirmPassword)}
                className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 cursor-pointer text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-700 transition-colors"
              >
                {showConfirmPassword ? (
                  <EyeOff className="w-5 h-5" />
                ) : (
                  <Eye className="w-5 h-5" />
                )}
              </div>
              {errors.confirmPassword && (
                <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-1">
                  {errors.confirmPassword}
                </p>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* N√∫t ƒëƒÉng k√Ω */}
            <button
              type="submit"
              disabled={loading}
              className={`w-full py-3 rounded-lg font-medium transition-all duration-200 flex items-center justify-center space-x-2 ${
                loading
                  ? "bg-gray-400 cursor-not-allowed"
                  : "bg-[#2A9D8F] hover:bg-[#228B7E] text-white shadow-md hover:shadow-lg"
              }`}
            >
              {loading ? (
                <>
                  <svg
                    className="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4 text-white"
                    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
                    fill="none"
                    viewBox="0 0 24 24"
                  >
                    <circle
                      className="opacity-25"
                      cx="12"
                      cy="12"
                      r="10"
                      stroke="currentColor"
                      strokeWidth="4"
                    ></circle>
                    <path
                      className="opacity-75"
                      fill="currentColor"
                      d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
                    ></path>
                  </svg>
                  <span>ƒêang t·∫°o t√†i kho·∫£n...</span>
                </>
              ) : (
                <span>T·∫°o t√†i kho·∫£n</span>
              )}
            </button>
          </form>

          <p className="text-sm text-center mt-6">
            ƒê√£ c√≥ t√†i kho·∫£n?{" "}
            <button
              onClick={() => navigate("/login")}
              className="text-[#2A9D8F] font-semibold hover:underline transition-all duration-200"
            >
              ƒêƒÉng nh·∫≠p ngay!
            </button>
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* B√™n tr√°i: Logo + m√¥ t·∫£ */}
      <div className="w-1/2 bg-[#E7F3F5] flex flex-col justify-center items-center">
        <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 md:p-6 lg:p-8 rounded-lg">
          <img
            src="/public/image/Xanh_d∆∞∆°ng_pastel_C·∫ßu_v·ªìng_Ch∆∞∆°ng_tr√¨nh_ƒê·ªçc_vi·∫øt_Logo-removebg-preview 1.png"
            alt="Logo"
            className="w-full h-auto object-contain max-w-full"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### src\pages\RegisterCustomer\index.tsx
```tsx
// pages/RegisterCustomer/index.tsx
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { User, Calendar, Users, Home } from "lucide-react";
import { useNavigate, useLocation } from "react-router-dom";
import { useDispatch } from "react-redux";
import type { AppDispatch, RootState } from "@/store/store";
import {
  registerCustomer,
  resetRegisterCustomerState,
} from "@/store/slices/registerCustomerSlice"; // ‚úÖ S·ª≠ d·ª•ng registerCustomerSlice
import { toast } from "react-toastify";
import { useSelector } from "react-redux";

export default function RegisterCustomerPage() {
  const [fullName, setFullName] = useState("");
  const [sex, setSex] = useState("");
  const [birthday, setBirthday] = useState("");
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState({
    fullName: "",
    sex: "",
    birthday: "",
  });

  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const location = useLocation();
  const dispatch = useDispatch<AppDispatch>();

  // ‚úÖ L·∫•y account data t·ª´ navigation state
  const accountData = location.state?.accountData;

  // L·∫•y state t·ª´ Redux store
  const { loading, success, error } = useSelector(
    (state: RootState) => state.registerCustomer // ‚úÖ S·ª≠ d·ª•ng registerCustomer state
  );

  // ‚úÖ Ki·ªÉm tra n·∫øu kh√¥ng c√≥ account data th√¨ redirect v·ªÅ register
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!accountData || !location.state?.fromRegister) {
      toast.error("Vui l√≤ng ƒëƒÉng k√Ω t√†i kho·∫£n tr∆∞·ªõc");
      navigate("/register");
      return;
    }
  }, [accountData, location.state, navigate]);

  // Cleanup khi component unmount
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      dispatch(resetRegisterCustomerState());
    };
  }, [dispatch]);

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω khi t·∫°o customer profile th√†nh c√¥ng
  useEffect(() => {
    if (success) {
      toast.success("T·∫°o h·ªì s∆° th√†nh c√¥ng! B·∫°n c√≥ th·ªÉ ƒëƒÉng nh·∫≠p ngay b√¢y gi·ªù.");
      setTimeout(() => {
        navigate("/login");
      }, 2000);
    }
  }, [success, navigate]);

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω khi c√≥ l·ªói t·ª´ server
  useEffect(() => {
    if (error) {
      toast.error(error.message);
    }
  }, [error]);

  const validateForm = () => {
    const newErrors = {
      fullName: "",
      sex: "",
      birthday: "",
    };
    let isValid = true;

    // Validate full name
    if (!fullName.trim()) {
      newErrors.fullName = "H·ªç v√† t√™n kh√¥ng ƒë∆∞·ª£c ƒë·ªÉ tr·ªëng";
      isValid = false;
    } else if (fullName.trim().length < 2) {
      newErrors.fullName = "H·ªç v√† t√™n ph·∫£i c√≥ √≠t nh·∫•t 2 k√Ω t·ª±";
      isValid = false;
    }

    // Validate sex
    if (!sex) {
      newErrors.sex = "Vui l√≤ng ch·ªçn gi·ªõi t√≠nh";
      isValid = false;
    }

    // Validate birthday
    if (!birthday) {
      newErrors.birthday = "Vui l√≤ng ch·ªçn ng√†y sinh";
      isValid = false;
    } else {
      const selectedDate = new Date(birthday);
      const today = new Date();
      if (selectedDate >= today) {
        newErrors.birthday = "Ng√†y sinh ph·∫£i tr∆∞·ªõc ng√†y h√¥m nay";
        isValid = false;
      }
    }

    setErrors(newErrors);
    return isValid;
  };

  const handleSubmit = async (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    // Validate form tr∆∞·ªõc khi submit
    if (!validateForm()) {
      return;
    }

    // ‚úÖ S·ª≠ d·ª•ng account_id t·ª´ accountData
    const account_id = accountData.id; // ho·∫∑c accountData.account_id t√πy thu·ªôc v√†o response structure

    // Format birthday to ISO string
    const birthdayISO = new Date(birthday).toISOString();

    // G·ª≠i request t·∫°o customer profile
    const customerData = {
      account_id: account_id,
      full_name: fullName.trim(),
      gender: sex,
      birthday: birthdayISO,
    };

    try {
      const result = await dispatch(registerCustomer(customerData));

      if (registerCustomer.fulfilled.match(result)) {
        console.log("‚úÖ T·∫°o customer profile th√†nh c√¥ng:", result.payload);
      } else if (registerCustomer.rejected.match(result)) {
        console.error("‚ùå T·∫°o customer profile th·∫•t b·∫°i:", result.payload);
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("‚ùå Unexpected error:", error);
      toast.error("C√≥ l·ªói kh√¥ng mong mu·ªën x·∫£y ra");
    }
  };

  // L·∫•y ng√†y hi·ªán t·∫°i ƒë·ªÉ l√†m max date cho birthday
  const getCurrentDate = () => {
    return new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
  };

  // ‚úÖ Kh√¥ng render n·∫øu kh√¥ng c√≥ account data
  if (!accountData) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex bg-white relative">
      {/* Icon quay v·ªÅ trang homepage */}
      <button
        onClick={() => navigate("/")}
        className="absolute top-4 right-4 text-[#2A9D8F] hover:text-[#228B7E] transition-colors duration-200 z-10"
        title="Quay l·∫°i trang ch√≠nh"
      >
        <Home className="w-6 h-6" />
      </button>

      {/* B√™n ph·∫£i: Form ƒëƒÉng k√Ω */}
      <div className="w-full md:w-1/2 flex items-center justify-center p-8">
        <div className="w-full max-w-sm bg-white p-8 rounded-xl shadow-lg border">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2 text-center">
            Ho√†n t·∫•t ƒëƒÉng k√Ω
          </h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-6 text-center">
            B∆∞·ªõc 2: T·∫°o h·ªì s∆° c√° nh√¢n cho{" "}
            <strong>{accountData.username}</strong>
          </p>

          <form className="space-y-4" onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
            {/* √î nh·∫≠p h·ªç v√† t√™n */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                value={fullName}
                onChange={(e) => setFullName(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="H·ªç v√† t√™n"
                className={`w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 transition-all duration-200 ${
                  errors.fullName
                    ? "border-red-500 focus:ring-red-500/20"
                    : "border-gray-300 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]/20 focus:border-[#2A9D8F]"
                }`}
                disabled={loading}
              />
              <User className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
              {errors.fullName && (
                <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-1">{errors.fullName}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* √î ch·ªçn gi·ªõi t√≠nh */}
            <div className="relative">
              <select
                value={sex}
                onChange={(e) => setSex(e.target.value)}
                className={`w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 transition-all duration-200 appearance-none ${
                  errors.sex
                    ? "border-red-500 focus:ring-red-500/20"
                    : "border-gray-300 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]/20 focus:border-[#2A9D8F]"
                }`}
                disabled={loading}
              >
                <option value="" disabled>
                  Ch·ªçn gi·ªõi t√≠nh
                </option>
                <option value="male">Nam</option>
                <option value="female">N·ªØ</option>
                <option value="other">Kh√°c</option>
              </select>
              <Users className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400 pointer-events-none" />
              {errors.sex && (
                <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-1">{errors.sex}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* √î ch·ªçn ng√†y sinh */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="date"
                value={birthday}
                onChange={(e) => setBirthday(e.target.value)}
                max={getCurrentDate()}
                className={`w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 transition-all duration-200 ${
                  errors.birthday
                    ? "border-red-500 focus:ring-red-500/20"
                    : "border-gray-300 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]/20 focus:border-[#2A9D8F]"
                }`}
                disabled={loading}
              />
              <Calendar className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400 pointer-events-none" />
              {errors.birthday && (
                <p className="text-red-500 text-xs mt-1">{errors.birthday}</p>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* N√∫t ho√†n t·∫•t */}
            <button
              type="submit"
              disabled={loading}
              className={`w-full py-3 rounded-lg font-medium transition-all duration-200 flex items-center justify-center space-x-2 ${
                loading
                  ? "bg-gray-400 cursor-not-allowed"
                  : "bg-[#2A9D8F] hover:bg-[#228B7E] text-white shadow-md hover:shadow-lg"
              }`}
            >
              {loading ? (
                <>
                  <svg
                    className="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4 text-white"
                    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
                    fill="none"
                    viewBox="0 0 24 24"
                  >
                    <circle
                      className="opacity-25"
                      cx="12"
                      cy="12"
                      r="10"
                      stroke="currentColor"
                      strokeWidth="4"
                    ></circle>
                    <path
                      className="opacity-75"
                      fill="currentColor"
                      d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
                    ></path>
                  </svg>
                  <span>ƒêang t·∫°o h·ªì s∆°...</span>
                </>
              ) : (
                <span>Ho√†n t·∫•t ƒëƒÉng k√Ω</span>
              )}
            </button>
          </form>

          <p className="text-sm text-center mt-6">
            ƒê√£ c√≥ t√†i kho·∫£n?{" "}
            <button
              onClick={() => navigate("/login")}
              className="text-[#2A9D8F] font-semibold hover:underline transition-all duration-200"
            >
              ƒêƒÉng nh·∫≠p ngay!
            </button>
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* B√™n tr√°i: Logo + m√¥ t·∫£ */}
      <div className="w-1/2 bg-[#E7F3F5] flex flex-col justify-center items-center">
        <div className="w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto p-4 md:p-6 lg:p-8 rounded-lg">
          <img
            src="/public/image/Xanh_d∆∞∆°ng_pastel_C·∫ßu_v·ªìng_Ch∆∞∆°ng_tr√¨nh_ƒê·ªçc_vi·∫øt_Logo-removebg-preview 1.png"
            alt="Logo"
            className="w-full h-auto object-contain max-w-full"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

```

### src\pages\RegisterShop\index.tsx
```tsx
// File: src/pages/RegisterPage.tsx (th√™m v√†o form ƒëƒÉng k√Ω)
import { useState } from "react";
import {
  User,
  Home,
  Store,
  Mail,
  Lock,
  Phone,
  MapPin,
  Briefcase,
  Clock,
  ChevronDown,
} from "lucide-react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";

export default function RegisterShop() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  interface FormData {
    businessName: string;
    businessAddress: string;
    phoneNumber: string;
    email: string;
    password: string;
    confirmPassword: string;
    businessFields: string[]; // Thay v√¨ never[]
    representativeName: string;
    workScheduleType: string;
    allWeekHours: {
      startTime: string;
      endTime: string;
    };
    customSchedule: {
      monday: { isWorking: boolean; startTime: string; endTime: string };
      tuesday: { isWorking: boolean; startTime: string; endTime: string };
      wednesday: { isWorking: boolean; startTime: string; endTime: string };
      thursday: { isWorking: boolean; startTime: string; endTime: string };
      friday: { isWorking: boolean; startTime: string; endTime: string };
      saturday: { isWorking: boolean; startTime: string; endTime: string };
      sunday: { isWorking: boolean; startTime: string; endTime: string };
    };
  }

  type DayKey =
    | "monday"
    | "tuesday"
    | "wednesday"
    | "thursday"
    | "friday"
    | "saturday"
    | "sunday";

  // S·ª≠ d·ª•ng interface trong useState
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<FormData>({
    businessName: "",
    businessAddress: "",
    phoneNumber: "",
    email: "",
    password: "",
    confirmPassword: "",
    businessFields: [] as string[], // Kh·ªüi t·∫°o ƒë√∫ng ki·ªÉu
    representativeName: "",
    workScheduleType: "",
    allWeekHours: {
      startTime: "08:00",
      endTime: "17:00",
    },
    customSchedule: {
      monday: { isWorking: true, startTime: "08:00", endTime: "17:00" },
      tuesday: { isWorking: true, startTime: "08:00", endTime: "17:00" },
      wednesday: { isWorking: true, startTime: "08:00", endTime: "17:00" },
      thursday: { isWorking: true, startTime: "08:00", endTime: "17:00" },
      friday: { isWorking: true, startTime: "08:00", endTime: "17:00" },
      saturday: { isWorking: true, startTime: "08:00", endTime: "14:00" },
      sunday: { isWorking: false, startTime: "08:00", endTime: "17:00" },
    },
  });

  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);
  const [showConfirmPassword, setShowConfirmPassword] = useState(false);
  // const [errors, setErrors] = useState({});

  // Danh s√°ch lƒ©nh v·ª±c kinh doanh
  const businessFieldOptions = [
    "Massage",
    "Grooming",
    "L∆∞u tr√∫",
    "D·ªãch v·ª• th√∫ y",
    "Hu·∫•n luy·ªán",
    "Ch·ª•p ·∫£nh",
    "T·ªï ch·ª©c ti·ªác",
    "ChƒÉm s√≥c ƒë·∫∑c bi·ªát",
  ];

  // Danh s√°ch c√°c ng√†y trong tu·∫ßn
  const daysOfWeek = [
    { key: "monday", label: "Th·ª© 2" },
    { key: "tuesday", label: "Th·ª© 3" },
    { key: "wednesday", label: "Th·ª© 4" },
    { key: "thursday", label: "Th·ª© 5" },
    { key: "friday", label: "Th·ª© 6" },
    { key: "saturday", label: "Th·ª© 7" },
    { key: "sunday", label: "Ch·ªß nh·∫≠t" },
  ];

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω thay ƒë·ªïi checkbox cho lƒ©nh v·ª±c kinh doanh
  const handleBusinessFieldChange = (field: string) => {
    setFormData((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      businessFields: prev.businessFields.includes(field)
        ? prev.businessFields.filter((f) => f !== field)
        : [...prev.businessFields, field],
    }));
  };

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω thay ƒë·ªïi input th√¥ng th∆∞·ªùng
  const handleInputChange = (e) => {
    const { name, value } = e.target;
    setFormData((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      [name]: value,
    }));
  };

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω thay ƒë·ªïi lo·∫°i l·ªãch l√†m vi·ªác
  const handleWorkScheduleTypeChange = (e) => {
    setFormData((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      workScheduleType: e.target.value,
    }));
  };

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω thay ƒë·ªïi gi·ªù l√†m vi·ªác to√†n tu·∫ßn
  const handleAllWeekHoursChange = (field, value) => {
    setFormData((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      allWeekHours: {
        ...prev.allWeekHours,
        [field]: value,
      },
    }));
  };

  // C·∫≠p nh·∫≠t function v·ªõi ƒë√∫ng ki·ªÉu
  const handleCustomScheduleChange = (
    day: DayKey,
    field: "isWorking" | "startTime" | "endTime",
    value: boolean | string
  ) => {
    setFormData((prev) => ({
      ...prev,
      customSchedule: {
        ...prev.customSchedule,
        [day]: {
          ...prev.customSchedule[day],
          [field]: value,
        },
      },
    }));
  };

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    console.log("Form data:", formData);
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex bg-white relative">
      {/* Icon quay v·ªÅ trang homepage */}
      <button
        onClick={() => navigate("/")}
        className="absolute top-4 right-4 text-[#2A9D8F] hover:text-[#228B7E] transition-colors duration-200 z-10"
        title="Quay l·∫°i trang ch√≠nh"
      >
        <Home className="w-6 h-6" />
      </button>

      {/* B√™n ph·∫£i: Form ƒëƒÉng k√Ω */}
      <div className="w-full md:w-1/2 flex items-center justify-center p-8 overflow-y-auto">
        <div className="w-full max-w-md bg-white p-8 rounded-xl shadow-lg border my-8">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2 text-center">
            ƒêƒÉng k√Ω c·ª≠a h√†ng
          </h2>
          <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mb-6 text-center">
            ƒêi·ªÅn th√¥ng tin ƒë·ªÉ ƒëƒÉng k√Ω t√†i kho·∫£n doanh nghi·ªáp
          </p>

          <form className="space-y-4" onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
            {/* T√™n doanh nghi·ªáp/c·ª≠a h√†ng */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                name="businessName"
                value={formData.businessName}
                onChange={handleInputChange}
                placeholder="T√™n doanh nghi·ªáp/T√™n c·ª≠a h√†ng"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F] focus:border-transparent"
                required
              />
              <Store className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
            </div>

            {/* ƒê·ªãa ch·ªâ doanh nghi·ªáp */}
            <div className="relative">
              <textarea
                name="businessAddress"
                value={formData.businessAddress}
                onChange={handleInputChange}
                placeholder="ƒê·ªãa ch·ªâ ƒë·∫ßy ƒë·ªß (s·ªë nh√†, t√™n ƒë∆∞·ªùng, ph∆∞·ªùng/x√£, qu·∫≠n/huy·ªán, t·ªânh/th√†nh ph·ªë)"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F] focus:border-transparent resize-none"
                rows="3"
                required
              />
              <MapPin className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
            </div>

            {/* S·ªë ƒëi·ªán tho·∫°i */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="tel"
                name="phoneNumber"
                value={formData.phoneNumber}
                onChange={handleInputChange}
                placeholder="S·ªë ƒëi·ªán tho·∫°i li√™n h·ªá ch√≠nh"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F] focus:border-transparent"
                required
              />
              <Phone className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
            </div>

            {/* Email */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="email"
                name="email"
                value={formData.email}
                onChange={handleInputChange}
                placeholder="Email li√™n h·ªá ch√≠nh"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F] focus:border-transparent"
                required
              />
              <Mail className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
            </div>

            {/* M·∫≠t kh·∫©u */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type={showPassword ? "text" : "password"}
                name="password"
                value={formData.password}
                onChange={handleInputChange}
                placeholder="M·∫≠t kh·∫©u (√≠t nh·∫•t 8 k√Ω t·ª±)"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F] focus:border-transparent"
                required
                minLength="8"
              />
              <div
                onClick={() => setShowPassword(!showPassword)}
                className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 cursor-pointer text-gray-500"
              >
                <Lock className="w-5 h-5" />
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* X√°c nh·∫≠n m·∫≠t kh·∫©u */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type={showConfirmPassword ? "text" : "password"}
                name="confirmPassword"
                value={formData.confirmPassword}
                onChange={handleInputChange}
                placeholder="Nh·∫≠p l·∫°i m·∫≠t kh·∫©u"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F] focus:border-transparent"
                required
              />
              <div
                onClick={() => setShowConfirmPassword(!showConfirmPassword)}
                className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 cursor-pointer text-gray-500"
              >
                <Lock className="w-5 h-5" />
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Lƒ©nh v·ª±c kinh doanh */}
            <div className="space-y-3">
              <label className="flex items-center text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">
                <Briefcase className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                Lƒ©nh v·ª±c kinh doanh (ch·ªçn nhi·ªÅu):
              </label>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 max-h-32 overflow-y-auto border rounded-lg p-3">
                {businessFieldOptions.map((field) => (
                  <label
                    key={field}
                    className="flex items-center space-x-2 text-sm"
                  >
                    <input
                      type="checkbox"
                      checked={formData.businessFields.includes(field)}
                      onChange={() => handleBusinessFieldChange(field)}
                      className="rounded border-gray-300 text-[#2A9D8F] focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]"
                    />
                    <span>{field}</span>
                  </label>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Ng√†y l√†m vi·ªác */}
            <div className="space-y-4">
              <label className="flex items-center text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">
                <Clock className="w-4 h-4 mr-2" />
                Ng√†y l√†m vi·ªác:
              </label>

              {/* Dropdown ch·ªçn lo·∫°i l·ªãch */}
              <div className="relative">
                <select
                  value={formData.workScheduleType}
                  onChange={handleWorkScheduleTypeChange}
                  className="w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F] focus:border-transparent appearance-none bg-white"
                  required
                >
                  <option value="">Ch·ªçn lo·∫°i l·ªãch l√†m vi·ªác</option>
                  <option value="all-week">To√†n b·ªô c√°c ng√†y trong tu·∫ßn</option>
                  <option value="custom">T√πy ch·ªânh</option>
                </select>
                <ChevronDown className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400 pointer-events-none" />
              </div>

              {/* Hi·ªÉn th·ªã component t∆∞∆°ng ·ª©ng */}
              {formData.workScheduleType === "all-week" && (
                <div className="border rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-50">
                  <h4 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-3">
                    Gi·ªù l√†m vi·ªác (√°p d·ª•ng cho t·∫•t c·∫£ c√°c ng√†y)
                  </h4>
                  <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
                    <div className="flex-1">
                      <label className="block text-xs text-gray-600 mb-1">
                        Gi·ªù b·∫Øt ƒë·∫ßu
                      </label>
                      <input
                        type="time"
                        value={formData.allWeekHours.startTime}
                        onChange={(e) =>
                          handleAllWeekHoursChange("startTime", e.target.value)
                        }
                        className="w-full px-3 py-2 border rounded focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]"
                      />
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500 mt-6">-</span>
                    <div className="flex-1">
                      <label className="block text-xs text-gray-600 mb-1">
                        Gi·ªù k·∫øt th√∫c
                      </label>
                      <input
                        type="time"
                        value={formData.allWeekHours.endTime}
                        onChange={(e) =>
                          handleAllWeekHoursChange("endTime", e.target.value)
                        }
                        className="w-full px-3 py-2 border rounded focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]"
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <p className="text-xs text-gray-500 mt-2">
                    V√≠ d·ª•: 8:00 - 17:00. Mu·ªën t√πy ch·ªânh chi ti·∫øt h∆°n, h√£y ch·ªçn
                    "T√πy ch·ªânh" ·ªü tr√™n.
                  </p>
                </div>
              )}

              {formData.workScheduleType === "custom" && (
                <div className="border rounded-lg p-4 bg-gray-50 space-y-3">
                  <h4 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-3">
                    T√πy ch·ªânh l·ªãch l√†m vi·ªác theo t·ª´ng ng√†y
                  </h4>
                  {daysOfWeek.map((day) => (
                    <div
                      key={day.key}
                      className="flex items-center space-x-3 p-3 bg-white rounded border"
                    >
                      <div className="w-20">
                        <span className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-700">
                          {day.label}
                        </span>
                      </div>

                      <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                        <input
                          type="checkbox"
                          checked={formData.customSchedule[day.key].isWorking}
                          onChange={(e) =>
                            handleCustomScheduleChange(
                              day.key,
                              "isWorking",
                              e.target.checked
                            )
                          }
                          className="rounded border-gray-300 text-[#2A9D8F] focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]"
                        />
                        <span className="text-xs text-gray-600">L√†m vi·ªác</span>
                      </div>

                      {formData.customSchedule[day.key].isWorking && (
                        <>
                          <div className="flex-1">
                            <input
                              type="time"
                              value={formData.customSchedule[day.key].startTime}
                              onChange={(e) =>
                                handleCustomScheduleChange(
                                  day.key,
                                  "startTime",
                                  e.target.value
                                )
                              }
                              className="w-full px-2 py-1 border rounded text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]"
                            />
                          </div>
                          <span className="text-gray-500 text-sm">-</span>
                          <div className="flex-1">
                            <input
                              type="time"
                              value={formData.customSchedule[day.key].endTime}
                              onChange={(e) =>
                                handleCustomScheduleChange(
                                  day.key,
                                  "endTime",
                                  e.target.value
                                )
                              }
                              className="w-full px-2 py-1 border rounded text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F]"
                            />
                          </div>
                        </>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            {/* T√™n ng∆∞·ªùi ƒë·∫°i di·ªán */}
            <div className="relative">
              <input
                type="text"
                name="representativeName"
                value={formData.representativeName}
                onChange={handleInputChange}
                placeholder="T√™n ng∆∞·ªùi ƒë·∫°i di·ªán/Ch·ªß doanh nghi·ªáp"
                className="w-full px-4 py-3 border rounded-lg pr-10 focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[#2A9D8F] focus:border-transparent"
                required
              />
              <User className="absolute top-3.5 right-3 w-5 h-5 text-gray-400" />
            </div>

            {/* N√∫t ƒëƒÉng k√Ω */}
            <button
              type="submit"
              className="w-full bg-[#2A9D8F] text-white py-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#228B7E] transition-all duration-200 font-medium shadow-md hover:shadow-lg"
            >
              ƒêƒÉng k√Ω t√†i kho·∫£n
            </button>
          </form>

          <p className="text-sm text-center mt-6">
            <a
              href="/login"
              className="text-[#2A9D8F] font-semibold hover:underline transition-all duration-200"
            >
              ƒê√£ c√≥ t√†i kho·∫£n? ƒêƒÉng nh·∫≠p ngay
            </a>
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
```

```tsx
import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { useParams, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import AppLayoutForUser from "../../layout/AppLayoutForUser";
import ServiceImages from "./components/ServiceImages";
import ServiceInfo from "./components/ServiceInfo";
import ServiceActions from "./components/ServiceActions";
import type { Service } from "@/types/services";

const mockService: Service = {
  id: "1",
  name: "C·∫Øt t·ªâa l√¥ng",
  images: [
    "/image/pet-grooming-1.jpg",
    "/image/pet-grooming-2.jpg",
    "/image/pet-grooming-3.jpg",
  ],
  rating: 5,
  reviewCount: 20,
  bookingCount: 100,
  category: "Grooming",
  originalPrice: 230000,
  currentPrice: 200000,
  discount: 15,
  petTypes: ["Th·ªè", "M√®o", "Ch√≥"],
  duration: 60,
  description: "D·ªãch v·ª• c·∫Øt t·ªâa l√¥ng chuy√™n nghi·ªáp cho th√∫ c∆∞ng...",
};

const ServiceDetail: React.FC = () => {
  const { id } = useParams<{ id: string }>();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [service, setService] = useState<Service | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchService = async () => {
      try {
        setLoading(true);
        setError(null);

        // Simulate API call v·ªõi mock data
        await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 1000)); // 1 gi√¢y ƒë·ªÉ test

        // Gi·∫£ l·∫≠p t√¨m service theo id
        if (id === "1" || id) {
          // Accept any id for demo
          setService(mockService);
        } else {
          setError("Service kh√¥ng t·ªìn t·∫°i");
        }
      } catch (err) {
        console.error("Error fetching service:", err);
        setError("C√≥ l·ªói x·∫£y ra khi t·∫£i d·ªØ li·ªáu");
      } finally {
        setLoading(false); // ‚úÖ Lu√¥n reset loading
      }
    };

    if (id) {
      fetchService();
    } else {
      setLoading(false);
      setError("Kh√¥ng c√≥ ID service");
    }
  }, [id]); // ‚úÖ Dependency array ƒë√∫ng

  const handleAddToCart = () => {
    console.log("Added to cart:", service?.id);
  };

  const handleBookNow = () => {
    if (service?.id) {
      navigate(`/booking/${service.id}`);
    }
  };

  // Loading state
  if (loading) {
    return (
      <AppLayoutForUser>
        <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-[400px]">
          <div className="text-center">
            <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-12 w-12 border-b-2 border-teal-600 mx-auto mb-4"></div>
            <p className="text-gray-600">ƒêang t·∫£i th√¥ng tin d·ªãch v·ª•...</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </AppLayoutForUser>
    );
  }

  // Error state
  if (error || !service) {
    return (
      <AppLayoutForUser>
        <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-[400px]">
          <div className="text-center">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900 mb-2">
              {error || "Kh√¥ng t√¨m th·∫•y d·ªãch v·ª•"}
            </h2>
            <p className="text-gray-600 mb-4">
              D·ªãch v·ª• b·∫°n t√¨m ki·∫øm kh√¥ng t·ªìn t·∫°i ho·∫∑c ƒë√£ b·ªã x√≥a.
            </p>
            <button
              onClick={() => navigate("/services")}
              className="px-4 py-2 bg-teal-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-teal-700"
            >
              Quay l·∫°i danh s√°ch d·ªãch v·ª•
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </AppLayoutForUser>
    );
  }

  // Success state
  return (
    <AppLayoutForUser>
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-gray-50">
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 py-8">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-8">
            <div>
              <ServiceImages
                images={service.images}
                serviceName={service.name}
              />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-6">
              <ServiceInfo service={service} />
              <ServiceActions
                onAddToCart={handleAddToCart}
                onBookNow={handleBookNow}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </AppLayoutForUser>
  );
};

export default ServiceDetail;
```

```tsx
import React, { useState } from "react";

interface ServiceImagesProps {
  images: string[];
  serviceName: string;
}

const ServiceImages: React.FC<ServiceImagesProps> = ({
  images,
  serviceName,
}) => {
  const [selectedImage, setSelectedImage] = useState(0);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {/* ·∫¢nh ch√≠nh */}
      <div className="aspect-square w-full overflow-hidden rounded-lg bg-gray-100">
        <img
          src={images[selectedImage]}
          alt={serviceName}
          className="h-full w-full object-cover"
        />
      </div>

      {/* ·∫¢nh thu nh·ªè */}
      <div className="flex space-x-2">
        {images.map((image, index) => (
          <button
            key={index}
            onClick={() => setSelectedImage(index)}
            className={`aspect-square w-20 overflow-hidden rounded-md border-2 ${
              selectedImage === index ? "border-orange-500" : "border-gray-200"
            }`}
          >
            <img
              src={image}
              alt={`${serviceName} ${index + 1}`}
              className="h-full w-full object-cover"
            />
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default ServiceImages;
```

### src\pages\Services\Service.tsx
```tsx
import React, { useState } from "react";
import { useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import FilterBar from "@/components/common/FilterBar";

// Mock data service
const mockServices = Array.from({ length: 12 }).map((_, idx) => ({
  id: idx + 1,
  name: "C·∫Øt t·ªâa l√¥ng",
  price: 200000,
  sold: 143,
  location: "H·ªì Ch√≠ Minh",
}));

const ServicesPage: React.FC = () => {
  const [services, setServices] = useState(mockServices);
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  // X·ª≠ l√Ω filter (hi·ªán t·∫°i ch·ªâ filter gi·∫£ l·∫≠p)
  const handleFilter = (filters: Record<string, string>) => {
    // TODO: Sau n√†y fetch API v·ªõi filters, hi·ªán t·∫°i ch·ªâ mock
    setServices(mockServices); // Gi·ªØ nguy√™n
  };

  // Khi click v√†o service
  const handleServiceClick = (id: number) => {
    navigate(`/service-detail/${id}`);
  };

  return (
    <div className="container mx-auto px-4 py-6">
      <FilterBar onFilter={handleFilter} />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4 mt-4">
        {services.map((service) => (
          <div
            key={service.id}
            onClick={() => handleServiceClick(service.id)}
            className="cursor-pointer bg-white rounded-lg shadow p-4 flex flex-col items-center hover:shadow-lg transition"
          >
            <div className="w-full h-28 bg-gray-100 rounded mb-3"></div>
            <div className="text-center">
              <div className="font-medium text-gray-800">{service.name}</div>
              <div className="text-orange-600 font-semibold mt-1">
                {service.price.toLocaleString()} ƒë
              </div>
              <div className="text-xs text-gray-400 mt-1">
                ƒê√£ b√°n: {service.sold} &nbsp;|&nbsp; {service.location}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default ServicesPage;
```

### src\pages\Shop\HotelRoomManagement.tsx

```tsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import type { Hotel, Room, HotelWithRooms } from '../../types/hotel';

const HotelManagement: React.FC = () => {
  const [hotels, setHotels] = useState<HotelWithRooms[]>([]);
  const [selectedHotel, setSelectedHotel] = useState<HotelWithRooms | null>(null);
  const [showHotelModal, setShowHotelModal] = useState(false);
  const [showRoomModal, setShowRoomModal] = useState(false);
  const [editingHotel, setEditingHotel] = useState<Hotel | null>(null);
  const [editingRoom, setEditingRoom] = useState<Room | null>(null);

  // Sample data
  const sampleHotels: HotelWithRooms[] = [
    {
      id: 1,
      name: 'Pet Paradise Hotel',
      description: 'Kh√°ch s·∫°n cao c·∫•p d√†nh cho th√∫ c∆∞ng',
      total_room: 20,
      available_room: 15,
      shop_id: 1,
      sub_address_id: 1,
      is_active: true,
      star: 5,
      rooms: [
        {
          id: 1,
          hotel_id: 1,
          room_number: 'A01',
          room_type: 'VIP',
          max_capability: 2,
          daily_price: 500000,
          is_available: true,
          amenities: 'ƒêi·ªÅu h√≤a, Camera, ƒê·ªì ch∆°i cao c·∫•p',
          star: 5
        },
        {
          id: 2,
          hotel_id: 1,
          room_number: 'B01',
          room_type: 'Standard',
          max_capability: 1,
          daily_price: 300000,
          is_available: false,
          amenities: 'Qu·∫°t, ƒê·ªì ch∆°i c∆° b·∫£n',
          star: 3
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      id: 2,
      name: 'Cozy Pet Inn',
      description: 'Kh√°ch s·∫°n ·∫•m c√∫ng cho th√∫ c∆∞ng nh·ªè',
      total_room: 15,
      available_room: 12,
      shop_id: 1,
      sub_address_id: 2,
      is_active: true,
      star: 4,
      rooms: []
    }
  ];

  useEffect(() => {
    setHotels(sampleHotels);
  }, []);

  const handleAddHotel = () => {
    setEditingHotel(null);
    setShowHotelModal(true);
  };

  const handleEditHotel = (hotel: Hotel) => {
    setEditingHotel(hotel);
    setShowHotelModal(true);
  };

  const handleDeleteHotel = (hotelId: number) => {
    if (confirm('B·∫°n c√≥ ch·∫Øc ch·∫Øn mu·ªën x√≥a kh√°ch s·∫°n n√†y?')) {
      setHotels(hotels.filter(h => h.id !== hotelId));
    }
  };

  const handleAddRoom = (hotel: HotelWithRooms) => {
    setSelectedHotel(hotel);
    setEditingRoom(null);
    setShowRoomModal(true);
  };

  const handleEditRoom = (room: Room) => {
    setEditingRoom(room);
    setShowRoomModal(true);
  };

  const handleDeleteRoom = (roomId: number) => {
    if (confirm('B·∫°n c√≥ ch·∫Øc ch·∫Øn mu·ªën x√≥a ph√≤ng n√†y?')) {
      setHotels(hotels.map(hotel => ({
        ...hotel,
        rooms: hotel.rooms.filter(r => r.id !== roomId)
      })));
    }
  };

  const getRoomTypeColor = (type: Room['room_type']) => {
    switch (type) {
      case 'VIP': return 'bg-purple-100 text-purple-800';
      case 'Suite': return 'bg-gold-100 text-gold-800';
      case 'Standard': return 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800';
      case 'Economy': return 'bg-green-100 text-green-800';
      default: return 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800';
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="p-6 bg-gray-50 min-h-screen">
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-8">
          <h1 className="text-3xl font-bold text-gray-900">
            Qu·∫£n l√Ω kh√°ch s·∫°n th√∫ c∆∞ng
          </h1>
          <button
            onClick={handleAddHotel}
            className="bg-teal-600 text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-teal-700 transition-colors"
          >
            + Th√™m kh√°ch s·∫°n m·ªõi
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* Danh s√°ch kh√°ch s·∫°n */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
          {hotels.map((hotel) => (
            <div key={hotel.id} className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-md overflow-hidden">
              {/* Header kh√°ch s·∫°n */}
              <div className="p-6 border-b border-gray-200">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                  <div>
                    <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold text-gray-900">{hotel.name}</h2>
                    <div className="flex items-center mt-1">
                      {[...Array(hotel.star)].map((_, i) => (
                        <span key={i} className="text-yellow-400">‚≠ê</span>
                      ))}
                      <span className="ml-2 text-sm text-gray-500">({hotel.star} sao)</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex space-x-2">
                    <button
                      onClick={() => handleEditHotel(hotel)}
                      className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800"
                    >
                      ‚úèÔ∏è
                    </button>
                    <button
                      onClick={() => handleDeleteHotel(hotel.id)}
                      className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800"
                    >
                      üóëÔ∏è
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>

                <p className="text-gray-600 text-sm mb-4">{hotel.description}</p>

                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm">
                  <div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500">T·ªïng ph√≤ng:</span>
                    <span className="ml-2 font-medium">{hotel.total_room}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="text-gray-500">Ph√≤ng tr·ªëng:</span>
                    <span className="ml-2 font-medium text-green-600">{hotel.available_room}</span>
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="mt-4">
                  <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${
                    hotel.is_active ? 'bg-green-100 text-green-800' : 'bg-red-100 text-red-800'
                  }`}>
                    {hotel.is_active ? 'Ho·∫°t ƒë·ªông' : 'T·∫°m d·ª´ng'}
                  </span>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Danh s√°ch ph√≤ng */}
              <div className="p-6">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">
                  <h3 className="text-lg font-medium text-gray-900">
                    Danh s√°ch ph√≤ng ({hotel.rooms.length})
                  </h3>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => handleAddRoom(hotel)}
                    className="bg-blue-600 text-white px-3 py-1 rounded text-sm hover:bg-blue-700 transition-colors"
                  >
                    + Th√™m ph√≤ng
                  </button>
                </div>

                {hotel.rooms.length > 0 ? (
                  <div className="space-y-3 max-h-60 overflow-y-auto">
                    {hotel.rooms.map((room) => (
                      <div key={room.id} className="border border-gray-200 rounded-lg p-3">
                        <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                          <div>
                            <h4 className="font-medium text-gray-900">
                              Ph√≤ng {room.room_number}
                            </h4>
                            <span className={`px-2 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${getRoomTypeColor(room.room_type)}`}>
                              {room.room_type}
                            </span>
                          </div>
                          <div className="flex space-x-2">
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleEditRoom(room)}
                              className="text-blue-600 hover:text-blue-800 text-sm"
                            >
                              ‚úèÔ∏è
                            </button>
                            <button
                              onClick={() => handleDeleteRoom(room.id)}
                              className="text-red-600 hover:text-red-800 text-sm"
                            >
                              üóëÔ∏è
                            </button>
                          </div>
                        </div>

                        <div className="text-xs text-gray-600 space-y-1">
                          <p>S·ª©c ch·ª©a: {room.max_capability} th√∫ c∆∞ng</p>
                          <p>Gi√°: {room.daily_price.toLocaleString('vi-VN')}ƒë/ng√†y</p>
                          <p>Ti·ªán nghi: {room.amenities}</p>
                          <p className={`${room.is_available ? 'text-green-600' : 'text-red-600'}`}>
                            {room.is_available ? 'C√≥ s·∫µn' : 'ƒê√£ ƒë·∫∑t'}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div className="text-center py-8 text-gray-500">
                    <p>Ch∆∞a c√≥ ph√≤ng n√†o</p>
                    <p className="text-sm">Nh·∫•n "Th√™m ph√≤ng" ƒë·ªÉ b·∫Øt ƒë·∫ßu</p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* Th·ªëng k√™ t·ªïng quan */}
        <div className="mt-8 grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4">
          <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-500">T·ªïng kh√°ch s·∫°n</h3>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-gray-900">{hotels.length}</p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-500">T·ªïng ph√≤ng</h3>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-blue-600">
              {hotels.reduce((sum, hotel) => sum + hotel.total_room, 0)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-500">Ph√≤ng tr·ªëng</h3>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-600">
              {hotels.reduce((sum, hotel) => sum + hotel.available_room, 0)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="bg-white p-4 rounded-lg shadow-md">
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-gray-500">T·ª∑ l·ªá l·∫•p ƒë·∫ßy</h3>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-purple-600">
              {hotels.length > 0 ? 
                Math.round(((hotels.reduce((sum, hotel) => sum + hotel.total_room, 0) - 
                hotels.reduce((sum, hotel) => sum + hotel.available_room, 0)) / 
                hotels.reduce((sum, hotel) => sum + hotel.total_room, 0)) * 100) : 0}%
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Modal th√™m/s·ª≠a kh√°ch s·∫°n */}
      {showHotelModal && (
        <HotelModal
          hotel={editingHotel}
          isOpen={showHotelModal}
          onClose={() => setShowHotelModal(false)}
          onSave={(hotelData) => {
            if (editingHotel) {
              // Update hotel
              setHotels(hotels.map(h => h.id === editingHotel.id ? { ...h, ...hotelData } : h));
            } else {
              // Add new hotel
              const newHotel: HotelWithRooms = {
                ...hotelData,
                id: Date.now(),
                rooms: []
              };
              setHotels([...hotels, newHotel]);
            }
            setShowHotelModal(false);
          }}
        />
      )}

      {/* Modal th√™m/s·ª≠a ph√≤ng */}
      {showRoomModal && (
        <RoomModal
          room={editingRoom}
          hotel={selectedHotel}
          isOpen={showRoomModal}
          onClose={() => setShowRoomModal(false)}
          onSave={(roomData) => {
            if (editingRoom) {
              // Update room
              setHotels(hotels.map(hotel => ({
                ...hotel,
                rooms: hotel.rooms.map(r => r.id === editingRoom.id ? { ...r, ...roomData } : r)
              })));
            } else {
              // Add new room
              const newRoom: Room = {
                ...roomData,
                id: Date.now(),
                hotel_id: selectedHotel!.id
              };
              setHotels(hotels.map(hotel => 
                hotel.id === selectedHotel!.id 
                  ? { ...hotel, rooms: [...hotel.rooms, newRoom] }
                  : hotel
              ));
            }
            setShowRoomModal(false);
          }}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
};
interface RoomModalProps {
  room: Room | null;
  hotel: HotelWithRooms | null;
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  onSave: (room: Omit<Room, 'id' | 'hotel_id'>) => void;
}

const RoomModal: React.FC<RoomModalProps> = ({ room, hotel, isOpen, onClose, onSave }) => {
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({
    room_number: '',
    room_type: 'Standard' as Room['room_type'],
    max_capability: 1,
    daily_price: 0,
    is_available: true,
    amenities: ''
    // B·ªè field star
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    if (room) {
      setFormData({
        room_number: room.room_number,
        room_type: room.room_type,
        max_capability: room.max_capability,
        daily_price: room.daily_price,
        is_available: room.is_available,
        amenities: room.amenities
        // B·ªè star: room.star
      });
    } else {
      setFormData({
        room_number: '',
        room_type: 'Standard',
        max_capability: 1,
        daily_price: 0,
        is_available: true,
        amenities: ''
        // B·ªè star: 3
      });
    }
  }, [room, isOpen]);


  useEffect(() => {
    if (room) {
      setFormData({
        room_number: room.room_number,
        room_type: room.room_type,
        max_capability: room.max_capability,
        daily_price: room.daily_price,
        is_available: room.is_available,
        amenities: room.amenities,
      });
    } else {
      setFormData({
        room_number: '',
        room_type: 'Standard',
        max_capability: 1,
        daily_price: 0,
        is_available: true,
        amenities: '',
      });
    }
  }, [room, isOpen]);

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    onSave(formData);
  };

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/30 flex items-center justify-center z-50 backdrop-blur-sm">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-xl p-6 w-full max-w-lg max-h-[90vh] overflow-y-auto shadow-2xl">
        <h2 className="text-xl font-semibold mb-4 text-gray-800">
          {room ? 'Ch·ªânh s·ª≠a ph√≤ng' : `Th√™m ph√≤ng m·ªõi - ${hotel?.name}`}
        </h2>
        
        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                S·ªë ph√≤ng *
              </label>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={formData.room_number}
                onChange={(e) => setFormData({...formData, room_number: e.target.value})}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
                placeholder="VD: A01"
                required
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                Lo·∫°i ph√≤ng
              </label>
              <select
                value={formData.room_type}
                onChange={(e) => setFormData({...formData, room_type: e.target.value as Room['room_type']})}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
              >
                <option value="Economy">Economy</option>
                <option value="Standard">Standard</option>
                <option value="Suite">Suite</option>
                <option value="VIP">VIP</option>
              </select>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                S·ª©c ch·ª©a *
              </label>
              <input
                type="number"
                value={formData.max_capability}
                onChange={(e) => setFormData({...formData, max_capability: parseInt(e.target.value) || 1})}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
                min="1"
                required
              />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
                Gi√°/ng√†y (VNƒê) *
              </label>
              <input
                type="number"
                value={formData.daily_price}
                onChange={(e) => setFormData({...formData, daily_price: parseInt(e.target.value) || 0})}
                className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
                min="0"
                required
              />
            </div>
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-1">
              Ti·ªán nghi
            </label>
            <textarea
              value={formData.amenities}
              onChange={(e) => setFormData({...formData, amenities: e.target.value})}
              className="w-full border border-gray-300 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 h-20 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-500 focus:border-blue-500"
              placeholder="VD: ƒêi·ªÅu h√≤a, Camera, ƒê·ªì ch∆°i..."
              rows={3}
            />
          </div>

          <div className="flex justify-end space-x-3 pt-4 border-t border-gray-200">
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={onClose}
              className="px-6 py-2.5 text-gray-600 bg-gray-100 border border-gray-300 rounded-lg hover:bg-gray-200 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-gray-300 transition-all duration-200 font-medium"
            >
              H·ªßy b·ªè
            </button>
            <button
              type="submit"
              className="px-6 py-2.5 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-blue-700 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-blue-300 transition-all duration-200 font-medium shadow-sm"
            >
              {room ? 'C·∫≠p nh·∫≠t' : 'Th√™m m·ªõi'}
            </button>
          </div>
        </form>
      </div>
    </div>
```
